<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">FOR IMMEDIATE RELEASE </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mar. 20, 2024 </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>General Mills Reports Fiscal 2024 Third-quarter Results </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net sales of $5.1&nbsp;billion were down 1&nbsp;percent in the third quarter and organic net sales<SUP
STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> were also down 1&nbsp;percent; on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis, net sales were up 6&nbsp;percent and organic net sales were up 7&nbsp;percent
</B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Operating profit of $911&nbsp;million was up 25&nbsp;percent; adjusted operating profit of $914&nbsp;million
increased 14&nbsp;percent in constant currency </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Diluted earnings per share (EPS) of $1.17 were up 27&nbsp;percent; adjusted diluted EPS of $1.17 increased
22&nbsp;percent in constant currency </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Company reaffirms full-year fiscal 2024 outlook </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>&sup1;</I></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><I>Please see Note 7 to the Consolidated Financial Statements below for reconciliation of this and other <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures used in this release. </I></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">MINNEAPOLIS (Mar. 20, 2024) &#150;
General Mills, Inc. (NYSE: GIS) today reported results for its fiscal 2024 third quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;General Mills&#146; strategic focus on
brand building, innovation, and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-store</FONT> execution contributed to improved volume and market share trends in the third quarter,&#148; said General Mills Chairman and Chief Executive Officer Jeff Harmening.
&#147;We continue to navigate today&#146;s evolving operating environment while generating industry-leading levels of cost savings. And we remain committed to investing further in our brands and capabilities to drive profitable growth over the long
term.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">General Mills is executing its Accelerate strategy to drive sustainable, profitable growth and
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-tier</FONT> shareholder returns over the long term. The strategy focuses on four pillars to create competitive advantages and win: boldly building brands, relentlessly innovating, unleashing scale, and standing
for good. The company is prioritizing its core markets, global platforms, and local gem brands that have the best prospects for profitable growth and is committed to reshaping its portfolio with strategic acquisitions and divestitures to further
enhance its growth profile. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Third Quarter Results Summary </U></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net sales</B> were down 1&nbsp;percent to $5.1&nbsp;billion, with lower pound volume partially offset by
favorable net price realization and mix. Organic net sales were 1&nbsp;percent below <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> results that grew double digits; organic net sales were up 7&nbsp;percent on a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Gross margin</B> was up 100 basis points to 33.5&nbsp;percent of net sales, driven by Holistic Margin
Management (HMM) cost savings, favorable net price realization and mix, and favorable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects, partially offset by higher other supply chain costs, input
cost inflation, and supply chain deleverage. Adjusted gross margin was up 20 basis points to 34.0&nbsp;percent of net sales, driven primarily by HMM cost savings and favorable net price realization and mix, partially offset by higher other supply
chain costs, input cost inflation, and supply chain deleverage. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Operating profit </B>of $911&nbsp;million was up 25&nbsp;percent, driven primarily by lower compensation and
benefits expenses, higher gross profit dollars, and product recall recoveries. <B>Operating profit margin</B> of 17.9&nbsp;percent was up 370 basis points. Adjusted operating profit of $914&nbsp;million increased 14&nbsp;percent in constant
currency, driven primarily by lower compensation and benefits expenses. Adjusted operating profit margin was up 220 basis points to 17.9&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net earnings attributable to General Mills</B> of $670&nbsp;million were up 21&nbsp;percent. <B>Diluted
EPS</B> was up 27&nbsp;percent to $1.17, driven primarily by higher operating profit and lower net shares outstanding, partially offset by higher net interest expense and a higher effective tax rate. Adjusted diluted EPS of $1.17 was up
22&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven primarily by higher adjusted operating profit, lower net shares outstanding, and a lower adjusted effective tax rate, partially offset by higher net interest expense. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Nine Month Results Summary </U></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net sales</B> increased 1&nbsp;percent to $15.1&nbsp;billion, with favorable net price realization and mix
partially offset by lower pound volume. Organic net sales were 1&nbsp;percent above <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> results that grew double digits; organic net sales were up 6&nbsp;percent on a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Gross margin</B> was up 260 basis points to 34.6&nbsp;percent of net sales, driven primarily by favorable net
price realization and mix, HMM cost savings, and favorable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects, partially offset by input cost inflation, higher other supply chain costs, and supply
chain deleverage. Adjusted gross margin was up 90 basis points to 34.8&nbsp;percent of net sales, driven by favorable net price realization and mix and HMM cost savings, partially offset by input cost inflation, higher other supply chain costs, and
supply chain deleverage. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Operating profit </B>of $2.65&nbsp;billion was up 1&nbsp;percent, driven primarily by higher gross profit
dollars, lower compensation and benefits expenses, and favorable net corporate investment activity, partially offset by net gains on divestitures in the prior year and a goodwill impairment charge.<B> Operating profit margin</B> of 17.5&nbsp;percent
was up 10 basis points. Adjusted operating profit of $2.8&nbsp;billion increased 9&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven by higher adjusted gross profit dollars and lower compensation and benefits expenses, partially offset by higher media and
other consumer expenses. Adjusted operating profit margin was up 150 basis points to 18.5&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net earnings attributable to General Mills</B> were down 2&nbsp;percent to $1.9&nbsp;billion. <B>Diluted
EPS</B> was up 2&nbsp;percent to $3.33, driven primarily by lower net shares outstanding and higher operating profit, partially offset by higher net interest expense. Adjusted diluted EPS of $3.51 was up 11&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven
primarily by higher adjusted operating profit, lower net shares outstanding, and a lower adjusted effective tax rate, partially offset by higher net interest expense. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Notes on Comparability </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following transactions
impacted the comparability of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-date</FONT></FONT> financial results between fiscal 2023 and fiscal 2024: the acquisition of the TNT Crust foodservice business in the first
quarter of fiscal 2023 and the divestiture of the Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes business in the first quarter of fiscal 2023. In addition, results in fiscal 2023 included the impact of a voluntary recall on certain international
<I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT></I> ice cream products, which was a headwind to net sales and operating profit results in the International segment. </P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>North America Retail Segment </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Third-quarter net sales for General Mills&#146; North America Retail segment of $3.2&nbsp;billion essentially matched
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> results, with favorable net price realization and mix offset by lower pound volume. Organic net sales were essentially in line with <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> results that grew
double digits; organic net sales were up 9&nbsp;percent on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis. Net sales performance outpaced Nielsen-measured retail sales growth in the quarter due primarily to an increase in
retailer inventory. Net sales were up <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">low-single</FONT> digits for the U.S. Morning Foods operating unit and were up high-single digits for Canada. Net sales were down
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">low-single</FONT> digits for U.S. Meals&nbsp;&amp; Baking Solutions and U.S. Snacks. Segment operating profit of $752&nbsp;million was down 4&nbsp;percent as reported and in constant currency, driven primarily by
higher other supply chain costs, input cost inflation, lower volume, and supply chain deleverage, partially offset by HMM cost savings and favorable net price realization and mix. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Through nine months, North America Retail segment net sales of $9.6&nbsp;billion essentially
matched <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> levels, including a modest headwind from divestitures. Organic net sales were up 1&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit of $2.4&nbsp;billion essentially matched <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> results as reported and in constant currency. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Pet Segment </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Third-quarter net sales for the Pet segment were down 3&nbsp;percent to $624&nbsp;million, driven by lower pound volume, partially offset by favorable net
price realization and mix. Organic net sales were 3&nbsp;percent below <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> results that grew double digits; organic net sales were up 5&nbsp;percent on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT>
compound growth basis. Net sales results in the quarter included declines on pet treats and dry pet food, partially offset by growth on wet pet food. Segment operating profit of $128&nbsp;million was up 25&nbsp;percent, driven primarily by HMM cost
savings and favorable net price realization and mix, partially offset by lower volume, higher selling, general, and administrative (SG&amp;A) expenses, and input cost inflation. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Through nine months, Pet segment net sales were down 2&nbsp;percent to $1.8&nbsp;billion. Organic net sales were also down 2&nbsp;percent.
Segment operating profit was up 10&nbsp;percent to $342&nbsp;million, driven primarily by favorable net price realization and mix and HMM cost savings, partially offset by lower volume, higher other supply chain costs, higher SG&amp;A expenses,
input cost inflation, and supply chain deleverage. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>North America Foodservice Segment </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Third-quarter net sales for the North America Foodservice segment increased 1&nbsp;percent to $552&nbsp;million. Organic net sales were also up 1&nbsp;percent
despite a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">4-point</FONT> headwind from market index pricing on bakery flour. Segment operating profit was down 1&nbsp;percent to $82&nbsp;million, driven primarily by higher other supply chain costs and higher
SG&amp;A expenses, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix and HMM cost savings. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Through nine months, North America
Foodservice net sales increased 3&nbsp;percent to $1.7&nbsp;billion, including a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-point</FONT> benefit from the TNT Crust acquisition. Organic net sales were up 1&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit was up
9&nbsp;percent to $236&nbsp;million, driven by favorable net price realization and mix and HMM cost savings, partially offset by higher other supply chain costs and higher SG&amp;A expenses. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>International Segment </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Third-quarter net sales for the
International segment were down 3&nbsp;percent to $680&nbsp;million, driven by lower pound volume. Organic net sales were also down 3&nbsp;percent, with declines in China and Brazil partially offset by growth in Europe&nbsp;&amp; Australia. Segment
operating profit totaled $18&nbsp;million compared to $42&nbsp;million a year ago, driven primarily by higher input costs and lower volume. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Through nine months, International net sales increased 3&nbsp;percent to $2.1&nbsp;billion, including a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-point</FONT> benefit from foreign currency exchange. Organic net sales were up 2&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit of $103&nbsp;million was up 8&nbsp;percent as reported and up 14&nbsp;percent in constant
currency from <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> results that included the impact of the ice cream recall, driven by favorable net price realization and mix and lower SG&amp;A expenses, partially offset by higher input costs and lower
volume. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Joint Venture Summary </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Third-quarter
constant-currency net sales increased 11&nbsp;percent for Cereal Partners Worldwide (CPW), driven by favorable net price realization and mix, partially offset by lower pound volume. Constant-currency net sales for
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT> Japan (HDJ) were down 2&nbsp;percent, driven by the timing of new product launches. Combined <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings from joint ventures of $18&nbsp;million
were up 42&nbsp;percent, driven by constant-currency <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings growth for CPW and HDJ, partially offset by unfavorable foreign currency exchange. Through nine months,
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings from joint ventures totaled $66&nbsp;million compared to $58&nbsp;million a year ago. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Other Income Statement Items </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Beginning this quarter, results from certain businesses managed by the company&#146;s Gold Medal Ventures entity are included in corporate and other net sales
and unallocated corporate items within operating profit. Unallocated corporate items also include corporate overhead expenses, variances to planned North American employee benefits and incentives, certain charitable contributions, restructuring
initiative project-related costs, gains and losses on corporate investments, and other items that are not part of the measurement of segment operating performance. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Third-quarter unallocated corporate items totaled $64&nbsp;million net expense in fiscal 2024 compared to $296&nbsp;million net expense a year
ago. Excluding <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation effects and other items affecting comparability, unallocated corporate items totaled $66&nbsp;million net expense this year
compared to $206&nbsp;million net expense last year, driven primarily by lower compensation and benefits expenses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Restructuring,
impairment, and other exit costs totaled $6&nbsp;million in the third quarter of fiscal 2024 compared to $1&nbsp;million a year ago <I>(please see Note 3 below for more information on these charges)</I>. Benefit plan
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-service</FONT> income totaled $19&nbsp;million in the third quarter compared to $22&nbsp;million a year ago, driven primarily by an increase in interest costs, partially offset by lower amortization of losses.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net interest expense totaled $122&nbsp;million in the third quarter of fiscal 2024 compared to $98&nbsp;million a year ago, driven
primarily by higher interest rates and higher average long-term debt levels. The effective tax rate in the quarter was 18.5&nbsp;percent compared to 16.6&nbsp;percent last year <I>(please see Note 6 below for more information on our effective tax
rate)</I>. The third-quarter adjusted effective tax rate was 18.4&nbsp;percent compared to 21.6&nbsp;percent a year ago, driven primarily by certain nonrecurring discrete tax benefits in the third quarter of fiscal 2024. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Cash Flow Generation and Cash Returns </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Cash
provided by operating activities totaled $2.4&nbsp;billion through nine months of fiscal 2024 compared to $2.0&nbsp;billion a year ago, driven primarily by higher net earnings excluding the net divestitures gain in fiscal 2023. Capital investments
totaled $486&nbsp;million compared to $351&nbsp;million a year ago. Dividends paid increased 6&nbsp;percent to $1.0&nbsp;billion. General Mills repurchased approximately 23.5&nbsp;million shares of common stock through nine months of fiscal 2024 for
a total of $1.6&nbsp;billion compared to $1.2&nbsp;billion in share repurchases a year ago. Average diluted shares outstanding through nine months decreased 3&nbsp;percent to 582&nbsp;million. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Fiscal 2024 Outlook </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">General Mills continues to
expect the largest factors impacting its performance in fiscal 2024 will be the economic health of consumers, the moderating rate of input cost inflation, and the increasing stability of the supply chain environment. Based on its current outlook on
these and other key factors, the company reaffirmed its full-year fiscal 2024 financial targets&sup2;: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

crusts for regional and national pizza chains, foodservice distributors, and retail outlets, for a purchase price of $253&nbsp;million. We financed the transaction with U.S. commercial paper. We consolidated the TNT Crust business into our
Consolidated Balance Sheets and recorded goodwill of $157&nbsp;million. The goodwill is included in the North America Foodservice segment and is not deductible for tax purposes. The pro forma effects of this acquisition were not material.

$9&nbsp;million of restructuring charges in the third quarter of fiscal 2024 and $14&nbsp;million of restructuring charges in the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;25, 2024, related to commercial strategy actions approved in the second quarter
of fiscal 2024. We recorded a $3&nbsp;million net recovery of restructuring charges in the third quarter of fiscal 2024 and $16&nbsp;million of restructuring charges in the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;25, 2024, related to restructuring
actions previously announced. We recorded $2&nbsp;million of restructuring charges in the third quarter of fiscal 2023 and $16&nbsp;million of restructuring charges in the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;26, 2023, related to restructuring
actions previously announced. We expect these actions to be completed by the end of fiscal 2026. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In the second quarter of fiscal 2024, we
recorded a $117&nbsp;million <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> goodwill impairment charge related to our Latin America reporting unit. </P>

we recorded a $26&nbsp;million net increase in expense related to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation of certain commodity positions and grain inventories, compared to a

of net losses in the third quarter of fiscal 2023. In the third quarter of fiscal 2024, we recorded $31&nbsp;million of net recoveries related to a voluntary recall on certain international
<I>H</I><I>&auml;</I><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">agen-Dazs</FONT></I> ice cream products in fiscal 2023, compared to a $1&nbsp;million charge in the same period last year. We recorded $1&nbsp;million of restructuring charges in cost of sales
in the third&nbsp;quarter of fiscal 2023. In addition, we recorded $1&nbsp;million of integration costs primarily related to our acquisition of TNT Crust in the third quarter of fiscal 2023. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Unallocated corporate expenses totaled $308&nbsp;million in the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;25, 2024, compared to $842&nbsp;million
in the same period last year. We recorded a $6&nbsp;million net increase in expense related to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation of certain commodity positions and grain
inventories in the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;25, 2024, compared to a $266&nbsp;million net increase in expense in the same period last year. In the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;25, 2024, certain compensation and benefits

2024, compared to $82&nbsp;million of net losses related to valuation adjustments and the sale of certain corporate investments in the same period last year. In the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;25, 2024, we recorded $31&nbsp;million of net
recoveries related to a voluntary recall on certain international <I>H</I><I>&auml;</I><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">agen-Dazs</FONT> </I>ice cream products in fiscal 2023, compared to a $26&nbsp;million charge in the same period last year. We
recorded $17&nbsp;million of restructuring charges and $2&nbsp;million of restructuring initiative project-related costs in cost of sales in the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;25, 2024, compared to $2&nbsp;million of restructuring charges in

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(6)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The effective tax rate for the third quarter of fiscal 2024 was 18.5&nbsp;percent compared to 16.6&nbsp;percent
for the third quarter of fiscal 2023. The 1.9 percentage point increase was primarily due to certain favorable tax components related to the divestitures in fiscal 2023, partially offset by certain nonrecurring discrete tax benefits in the third
quarter of fiscal 2024. Our effective tax rate excluding certain items affecting comparability was 18.4&nbsp;percent in the third quarter of fiscal 2024, compared to 21.6&nbsp;percent in the same period last year (see Note 7 below for a description
of our use of measures not defined by GAAP). The 3.2 percentage point decrease was primarily due to certain nonrecurring discrete tax benefits in the third quarter of fiscal 2024. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The effective tax rate for the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;25, 2024, was 19.5&nbsp;percent compared to 19.6&nbsp;percent for the
nine-month period ended February&nbsp;26, 2023. The 0.1 percentage point decrease was primarily due to certain nonrecurring discrete tax benefits in fiscal 2024, partially offset by certain favorable tax components related to the divestitures in
fiscal 2023. Our effective tax rate excluding certain items affecting comparability was 20.1&nbsp;percent in the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;25, 2024, compared to 20.8&nbsp;percent in the same period last year (see Note 7 below for a
description of our use of measures not defined by GAAP). The 0.7 percentage point decrease was primarily due to certain nonrecurring discrete tax benefits in fiscal 2024. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(7)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">We have included measures in this release that are not defined by GAAP. We believe that these measures provide
useful information to investors, and include these measures in other communications to investors. For each of these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, we are providing below a reconciliation of the differences
between the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure and the most directly comparable GAAP measure, an explanation of why we believe the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure provides useful information to
investors and any additional material purposes for which our management or Board of Directors uses the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure. These <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures should be viewed in
addition to, and not in lieu of, the comparable GAAP measure. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We provide organic net sales growth rates for our consolidated net sales and segment net
sales. This measure is used in reporting to our Board of Directors and executive management and as a component of the Board of Directors&#146; measurement of our performance for incentive compensation purposes. We believe that organic net sales
growth rates provide useful information to investors because they provide transparency to underlying performance in our net sales by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations, acquisitions, divestitures, and a
53rd&nbsp;fiscal week, when applicable, have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability. A reconciliation of these measures to reported net sales growth rates, the relevant GAAP
measures, are included in our Operating Segment Results above. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Certain measures in this release are presented excluding the impact of
foreign currency exchange (constant-currency). To present this information, current period results for entities reporting in currencies other than United States dollars are translated into United States dollars at the average exchange rates in
effect during the corresponding period of the prior fiscal year, rather than the actual average exchange rates in effect during the current fiscal year. Therefore, the foreign currency impact is equal to current year results in local currencies
multiplied by the change in the average foreign currency exchange rate between the current fiscal period and the corresponding period of the prior fiscal year. We believe that these constant-currency measures provide useful information to investors
because they provide transparency to underlying performance by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">period-to-period</FONT></FONT>
comparability given volatility in foreign currency exchange markets. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our fiscal 2024 outlook for organic net sales growth, adjusted
operating profit growth, adjusted diluted EPS growth, and free cash flow conversion are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures that exclude, or have otherwise been adjusted for, items impacting comparability, including
the effect of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations, acquisitions, divestitures, and a 53rd week, when applicable. We are not able to reconcile these forward-looking <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures to their
most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measure without unreasonable efforts because we are unable to predict with a reasonable degree of certainty the actual impact of changes in foreign currency exchange rates or the timing of
acquisitions and divestitures throughout fiscal 2024. The unavailable information could have a significant impact on our fiscal 2024 GAAP financial results. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For fiscal 2024, we currently expect: foreign currency exchange rates (based on a blend of forward and forecasted rates and hedge positions)
and acquisitions and divestitures will have no material impact to net sales growth and restructuring charges to total approximately $45&nbsp;million to $50&nbsp;million. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Significant Items Impacting Comparability </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Several measures below are presented on an adjusted basis. The adjustments are either items resulting from infrequently occurring events or items that, in
management&#146;s judgement, significantly affect the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> assessment of operating results. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following are descriptions of significant items impacting comparability of our results. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Goodwill impairment</U> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-cash</FONT> goodwill impairment charge related to our Latin America reporting unit in fiscal 2024. Please see Note 3. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Product recall, net</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Costs related to the fiscal 2023 voluntary recall of certain international <I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT></I> ice
cream products, net of recoveries. Please see Note 4. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Restructuring charges and project-related costs</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Restructuring charges and project-related costs related to commercial strategy restructuring actions and previously announced restructuring
actions recorded in fiscal 2024. Restructuring charges for previously announced restructuring actions recorded in fiscal 2023. Please see Note 3. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Investment activity, net</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Valuation adjustments of certain corporate investments in fiscal 2024. Valuation adjustments and the loss on sale of certain corporate
investments in fiscal 2023. Please see Note 4. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation of certain commodity positions
recognized in unallocated corporate items. Please see Note 4. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Transaction costs</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Immaterial transaction costs incurred in fiscal 2024. Transaction costs primarily related to the sale of our Helper main meals and Suddenly
Salad side dishes business in fiscal 2023. Please see Note 2. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Acquisition integration costs</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Integration costs primarily resulting from the acquisition of TNT Crust in fiscal 2024 and fiscal 2023. Please see Note 2. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Divestitures gain, net</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net divestitures gain primarily related to the sale of our Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes business in fiscal 2023. Please see
Note 2. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>CPW restructuring charges</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">CPW restructuring charges related to previously announced restructuring actions. </P>
</DIV></Center>

<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Adjusted Operating Profit Growth on a Constant-currency Basis </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This measure is used in reporting to our Board of Directors and executive management and as a component of the measurement of our performance for incentive
compensation purposes. We believe that this measure provides useful information to investors because it is the operating profit measure we use to evaluate operating profit performance on a comparable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> basis. The measure is evaluated on a constant-currency basis by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability given the volatility in foreign currency exchange rates.&#8195; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our adjusted
operating profit growth on a constant-currency basis is calculated as follows: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Adjusted Effective Income Tax Rate </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We believe this measure provides useful information to investors because it presents the adjusted effective income tax rate on a comparable <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted effective income tax rates are calculated as
follows: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" ALIGN="center">
